# Text Elements
the certification is not our target 
but the knowledge is. ^O8pGGDly

Kubernetes and Cloud Native Associate (KCNA) ^KGwOWqrA

The Kubernetes and Cloud Native Associate (KCNA) exam demonstrates 
a user’s foundational knowledge and skills in Kubernetes and the wider cloud 
native ecosystem. ^gB9wm13t

Exam details ^HE9JcdrM

The certification exam tests specific domains and competencies including: ^H5eq8A45

DOMAIN                          WEIGHT ^kIpTU4mq

Cloud Native Architecture                16% ^vJ8wmedr

Cloud Native Observability                8% ^CaOZ5fde

Cloud Native Application Delivery          8% ^cTEuIXfT
